msg:The hotel is great overall, with the best service, but it is inconvenient to travel. 1. The hotel is in a great location, just opposite the scenic spot, and you can see across the river. You can see the Guangji Bridge while sitting in the room. 2. The service attitude is excellent. Whether it is the front desk service, customer service or restaurant service, every service staff is very polite and takes the initiative to introduce the situation to the guests. Among them, I would like to especially thank the front desk waiter Miss Li, who is warm and thoughtful in receiving guests, treating guests like relatives and friends, and can take the initiative to help guests solve various problems. 3. The service is personalized. The hotel provides a 100 yuan breakfast voucher, which can be ordered by yourself or eaten at the buffet for free. This is the first time I have encountered this. It is very personalized and fully meets the tastes of different guests. I stayed in the hotel for three days, ordered my own food for two days, and had a buffet on the last day to catch the train. The breakfast was very good. 4. The hotel is in an excellent location, but it is inconvenient to go to the scenic spots. It is not a hotel problem, but mainly a shortcoming of urban construction. There is no subway and no bus. This is a strange thing. Although Gaode Map shows that there are bus routes, they are not in operation time, which is equivalent to no bus. You either have your own car or take a taxi. Every time you go to the scenic spot, it costs more than 20 yuan (one way). It is difficult to get a taxi around 15:30 in the afternoon. Basically no one accepts the order. You can only increase the price. It costs 70 yuan for a car to accept the order. In addition, the one-way taxi from the hotel to the railway station is about 68 yuan. It is said that Chaoshan is already building a subway, and it is expected to take another three years, that is, 2027. 5. There is no safe in the hotel room, which is not convenient for guests to store valuables. They can only carry them with them every day. It is recommended to add it if conditions permit, at least for deluxe rooms and above. In addition, there is no scale in the room. It is recommended to add it. People nowadays attach great importance to their health.
